               <h4 class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title">
                <a class="ui--a articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link" data-kanal-page="dunia" data-template-var="url" href="https://www.bola.com/dunia/read/3603140/betah-di-as-roma-el-shaarawy-tolak-pendekatan-torino" title="Betah di AS Roma, El Shaarawy Tolak Pendekatan Torino">
                 <span class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link-text" data-template-var="title">
                  Betah di AS Roma, El Shaarawy Tolak Pendekatan Torino
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h4>
              </header>
              <div class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__summary" data-template-var="summary">
               El Shaarawy enggan tinggalkan AS Roma.
              </div>

               <h4 class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title">
                <a class="ui--a articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link" data-kanal-page="asian-games" data-template-var="url" href="https://www.bola.com/asian-games/read/3603011/china-menargetkan-10-medali-emas-dari-loncat-indah-di-asian-games-2018" title="China Menargetkan 10 Medali Emas dari Loncat Indah di Asian Games 2018">
                 <span class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link-text" data-template-var="title">

                 </span>
                </a>
               </h4>
              </header>
              <div class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__summary" data-template-var="summary">

               <h4 class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title">
                <a class="ui--a articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link" data-kanal-page="indonesia" data-template-var="url" href="https://www.bola.com/indonesia/read/3603105/masih-cedera-otavio-dutra-ingin-tampil-pada-laga-persebaya-vs-persela" title="Masih Cedera, Otavio Dutra Ingin Tampil pada Laga Persebaya Vs Persela">
                 <span class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link-text" data-template-var="title">
                  Masih Cedera, Otavio Dutra Ingin Tampil pada Laga Persebaya Vs Persela

               Stoper Persebaya Surabaya, Otavio Dutra masih dibekap cedera hamstring.

               <h4 class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title">

                 </span>
                </a>
               </h4>
              </header>

               Barcelona sudah mencatat beberapa kontroversi pada aktivitas transfer.

               <h4 class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title">
                <a class="ui--a articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link" data-kanal-page="indonesia" data-template-var="url" href="https://www.bola.com/indonesia/read/3603099/psis-menunggu-nur-iskandar" title="PSIS Menunggu Nur Iskandar">
                 <span class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__title-link-text" data-template-var="title">
                  PSIS Menunggu Nur Iskandar
                 </span>
                </a>
               </h4>
              </header>
              <div class="articles--iridescent-list--text-item__summary" data-template-var="summary">
               PSIS Semarang selangkah lagi mendapatkan pemain tambahan untuk mengarungi putaran kedua Gojek Liga 1 bersama Bukalapak.
              </div>

               Pelatih Persela, Aji Santoso, menyebut kehadiran Dendy Sulistyawan bisa semakin menambah variasi serangan tim asuhannya,
              </div>

 /*** START of #155541245 Tracking GTM bola net impression ****/
 function isInViewport($selector) {
 	var scrollPos = $(window).scrollTop();
 	var bottomPos = scrollPos + $(window).height();
 	var elementTopPos = $selector.offset().top;
 	var elementBottomPos = $selector.offset().top + $selector.height();
 
 	return (bottomPos > elementTopPos && elementTopPos > scrollPos) ||
   	(bottomPos > elementBottomPos && elementBottomPos > scrollPos) ||
 		(scrollPos > elementTopPos && bottomPos < elementBottomPos);
 }
 
 var dataImpression = {
   "event": "impression",
 	"feature_location": "sidebar",
 	"feature_name": "widget-gateway",
 };
 
 var hasSendImpressionBolaNet = false;
 
 // GTM Impression
 window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
   var contentPayment = $('.bola-net-widget');
 	if (contentPayment.length > 0 && isInViewport(contentPayment) && !hasSendImpressionBolaNet) {
     window.dataLayer.push(dataImpression);
     hasSendImpressionBolaNet = true;
   }
 }.bind(this));
 /*** END of #155541245 Tracking GTM bola net impression ****/

 	      lb_def = googletag.defineSlot('/36504930/www.bola.com/dfp-lb', [[970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], 'div-gpt-ad-bolacom-lb').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting("leaderboard_type", dfp_lb_keyTargetting);
 	      googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bolacom-lb');
 	      googletag.pubads().refresh([lb_def]);
 	      //CriteoCDBRefreshDFP([lb_def]);
 	  } 
 	  /* END LB AND BILLBOARD RENDERRING */
 	  
 	  /* DISPLAY NONE THE IFRAME, FOR ADS ELEMENT OUTSIDE IT'S IFRAME CONTAINER */
 	  if (dfp_slotElementId.match(/-oop/) && !dfp_slotElementId.match(/billboard/)) {
             if (document.getElementById(dfp_slotElementId).getElementsByTagName('iframe')[0].getAttribute('height') == 1) {
                 document.getElementById(dfp_slotElementId).getElementsByTagName('iframe')[0].style.display = "none";
             }
 	  }
 	});
 	
 	/*GET META*/
 	function document_meta(metaName) {
         var metaResult = '';
         var metas = document.getElementsByTagName('meta');
         if (metas) {
             for (var x = 0, y = metas.length; x < y; x++) {
                 if (metas[x].name.toLowerCase() == metaName) {
                     metaResult += metas[x].content;
                 }
             }
         }
         return metaResult != '' ? metaResult : '';
     }
 	
 	function inArray(needle, haystack) {
         var length = haystack.length;
         for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
             if (haystack[i] == needle) return true;
         }
         return false;
     }

 	googletag.pubads().setTargeting("Site", "BOLA.COM");

 	googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);
 	googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
